const getPIN = (w) => { let h = (w ^ 0xdeadbeef) >>> 0; h = Math.imul(h ^ (h >>> 16), 0x45d9f3b) >>> 0; h = Math.imul(h ^ (h >>> 16), 0x45d9f3b) >>> 0; return String(100000 + ((h ^ (h >>> 16)) >>> 0) % 900000).padStart(6, "0"); }; const getCW = () => Math.floor(Date.now() / 60000); const getSecsLeft = () => 60 - (Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) % 60); const pad = n => String(n).padStart(2, "0"); const todayStr = () => { const d = new Date(); return `${d.getFullYear()}-${pad(d.getMonth()+1)}-${pad(d.getDate())}`; }; const fmtTime = iso => { if (!iso) return "--:--"; const d = new Date(iso); return `${pad(d.getHours())}:${pad(d.getMinutes())}`; }; const fmtDate = iso => { if (!iso) return ""; const d = new Date(iso); return `${pad(d.getDate())}/${pad(d.getMonth()+1)}/${d.getFullYear()}`; }; const diffMin = (a, b) => (!a || !b) ? 0 : Math.round((new Date(b) - new Date(a)) / 60000); const toHHMM = m => { const s = m < 0 ? "-" : "+"; const a = Math.abs(m); return `${s}${pad(Math.floor(a/60))}:${pad(a%60)}`; }; const MONTHS = ["Enero","Febrero","Marzo","Abril","Mayo","Junio","Julio","Agosto","Septiembre","Octubre","Noviembre","Diciembre"]; // Returns expected minutes for a given date string "YYYY-MM-DD" based on employee schedule // Returns 0 if it's Sunday or the employee doesn't work that day const getExpectedMin = (emp, dateStr) => { const d = new Date(dateStr + "T12:00:00"); const dow = d.getDay(); // 0=Sun,1=Mon,...,6=Sat if (dow === 0) return 0; // domingo if (dow === 6) return emp.schedule ? emp.schedule.sat : 0; return emp.schedule ? emp.schedule.wday : (emp.hoursPerDay || 8) * 60; }; // Returns formatted schedule string for display const fmtSchedule = (emp) => { if (!emp.schedule) return emp.position || ""; const wh = emp.schedule.wday / 60; const sh = emp.schedule.sat / 60; if (sh > 0) return `Lun-Vie ${wh}h / Sáb ${sh}h`; return `Lun-Vie ${wh}h`; }; // "exempt" event types that skip the day's expected hours const EXEMPT_TYPES = new Set(["vacation","franco","solicitud","dia_especial"]); // schedule: wday = minutos Lun-Vie, sat = minutos Sábado (0 = no trabaja sábados) const DEFAULT_DATA = { employees: [ { id:"AF001", name:"Agustín Faró", schedule:{ wday:9*60, sat:0 } }, { id:"AG002", name:"Ariel González", schedule:{ wday:8*60, sat:5*60 } }, { id:"LL003", name:"Luciana López", schedule:{ wday:9*60, sat:0 } }, { id:"AB004", name:"Agustina Billalva", schedule:{ wday:8*60, sat:5*60 } }, { id:"RO005", name:"Rodrigo", schedule:{ wday:4*60, sat:0 } }, { id:"NA006", name:"Nahuel Arias Escudero", schedule:{ wday:8*60, sat:5*60 } }, { id:"MA007", name:"Maximiliano Arias", schedule:{ wday:8*60, sat:5*60 } }, { id:"IR008", name:"Ignacio Risso", schedule:{ wday:8*60, sat:5*60 } }, { id:"AM009", name:"Agustín Muschiato", schedule:{ wday:8*60, sat:5*60 } }, { id:"PG010", name:"Pablo Gianini", schedule:{ wday:8*60, sat:5*60 } }, { id:"MB011", name:"Mauricio Bustos", schedule:{ wday:8*60, sat:5*60 } }, ], records: [], events: [], }; // ── QR Display (loads qrcode.js from CDN safely) ──────────── function QRDisplay() { const canvasRef = useState(null); const [ready, setReady] = useState(false); const [err, setErr] = useState(false); s.src = "https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/qrcodejs/1.0.0/qrcode.min.js"; s.onload = () => { setReady(true); }; s.onerror = () => setErr(true); document.head.appendChild(s); }, []); useEffect(() => { if (!ready) return; const el = document.getElementById("qr-canvas-kiosk"); if (!el || !window.QRCode) return; el.innerHTML = ""; try { new window.QRCode(el, { text: "https://attendance.app/fichar", width: 180, height: 180, colorDark: "#60a5fa", colorLight: "#0d0d12", correctLevel: window.QRCode.CorrectLevel.M, }); } catch(e) { setErr(true); } }, [ready]); if (err) return (

); } // ── CSV export ─────────────────────────────────────────────── function exportCSV(rows, filename) { const csv = rows.map(r => r.map(c => `"${String(c ?? JSON.parse(r.value) : DEFAULT_DATA)) .catch(() => setData(DEFAULT_DATA)); }, []); // Save useEffect(() => { if (data) window.storage.set(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(data)).catch(() => {}); }, [data]); // Tick useEffect(() => { const t = setInterval(() => { setClock(new Date()); setSecs(getSecsLeft()); setPin(getPIN(getCW())); }, 1000); return () => clearInterval(t); }, []); if (!data) return (
CARGANDO...
); // ── Data helpers ───────────────────────────────────────── const today = todayStr(); const getEmp = id => data.employees.find(e => e.id === id); const getRec = id => data.records.find(r => r.empId === id && r.date === today); const getEvts = id => data.events.filter(e => e.empId === id); const getStats = (id, filterRecs, filterEvts) => { const emp = getEmp(id); const recs = (filterRecs || data.records).filter(r => r.empId === id && r.checkIn && r.checkOut); const evts = (filterEvts || data.events).filter(e => e.empId === id && EXEMPT_TYPES.has(e.type)); // Build set of exempt dates (franco, vacaciones, solicitud, dia_especial) const exemptDates = new Set(); evts.forEach(e => { if (e.dateTo) { // range — add each day let cur = new Date(e.date + "T12:00:00"); const end = new Date(e.dateTo + "T12:00:00"); while (cur <= end) { exemptDates.add(cur.toISOString().slice(0,10)); cur.setDate(cur.getDate() + 1); } } else if (e.date) { exemptDates.add(e.date); } }); let totalWorked = 0; let totalExpected = 0; recs.forEach(r => { const worked = diffMin(r.checkIn, r.checkOut); totalWorked += worked; if (!exemptDates.has(r.date)) { totalExpected += getExpectedMin(emp, r.date); } }); return { total:totalWorked, expected:totalExpected, balance:totalWorked - totalExpected, days:recs.length }; }; const getMonthRecs = (id, y, m) => data.records.filter(r => { if (r.empId !== id) return false; const [ry, rm] = r.date.split("-"); return parseInt(ry) === y && parseInt(rm) - 1 === m; }); const getMonthEvts = (id, y, m) => data.events.filter(e => { if (e.empId !== id || !e.date) return false; const [ey, em] = e.date.split("-"); return parseInt(ey) === y && parseInt(em) - 1 === m; }); // ── Actions ────────────────────────────────────────────── const handleCheckin = () => { setFeedback(null); const emp = data.employees.find(e => e.id === empCode.toUpperCase().trim()); if (!emp) { setFeedback({ ok:false, msg:"Código de empleado no encontrado." }); return; } const valid = [getPIN(getCW()), getPIN(getCW() - 1)]; if (!valid.includes(entPin.trim())) { setFeedback({ ok:false, msg:"PIN incorrecto. Mirá la pantalla del local." }); return; } const rec = getRec(emp.id); if (ciAction === "in") { if (rec) { setFeedback({ ok:false, msg:"Ya registraste tu entrada hoy." }); return; } const now = new Date().toISOString(); setData(d => ({ ...d, records:[...d.records, { id:Date.now(), empId:emp.id, date:today, checkIn:now, checkOut:null }] })); setFeedback({ ok:true, msg:`¡Bienvenida/o, ${emp.name}! Entrada a las ${fmtTime(now)}.` }); } else { if (!rec) { setFeedback({ ok:false, msg:"No hay entrada registrada hoy." }); return; } if (rec.checkOut) { setFeedback({ ok:false, msg:"Ya registraste tu salida hoy." }); return; } const now = new Date().toISOString(); setData(d => ({ ...d, records:d.records.map(r => r.id === rec.id ? { ...r, checkOut:now } : r) })); const w = diffMin(rec.checkIn, now); setFeedback({ ok:true, msg:`¡Hasta pronto, ${emp.name}! Salida ${fmtTime(now)}. Trabajaste ${Math.floor(w/60)}h ${w%60}m.` }); } setEmpCode(""); setEntPin(""); }; const openEvtModal = (empId) => { setEvtModal(empId); setEvtType("vacation"); setEvtDate(""); setEvtDateTo(""); setEvtByTime(true); setEvtFrom(""); setEvtTo(""); setEvtHours(""); setEvtNote(""); }; const saveEvent = () => { if (!evtDate) return; let hours = evtHours; if (evtType === "tramite" && evtByTime && evtFrom && evtTo) { const [hf, mf] = evtFrom.split(":").map(Number); const [ht, mt] = evtTo.split(":").map(Number); const mins = (ht * 60 + mt) - (hf * 60 + mf); if (mins > 0) hours = `${Math.floor(mins/60)}h${mins % 60 > 0 ? ` ${mins%60}m` : ""}`; } const evt = { id:Date.now(), empId:evtModal, type:evtType, date:evtDate, dateTo:evtDateTo, timeFrom:evtFrom, timeTo:evtTo, hours, note:evtNote }; setData(d => ({ ...d, events:[...d.events, evt] })); setEvtModal(null); }; const delEvent = id => setData(d => ({ ...d, events:d.events.filter(e => e.id !== id) })); const saveEmployee = () => { if (!neId || !neName) return; const emp = { id:neId.toUpperCase(), name:neName, schedule:{ wday:Math.round(Number(neHrs)*60), sat:Math.round(Number(neSat)*60) } }; setData(d => ({ ...d, employees:[...d.employees, emp] })); setNewEmpM(false); setNeId(""); setNeName(""); setNePos(""); setNeHrs("8"); setNeSat("0"); }; const doEmpCSV = id => { const emp = getEmp(id); const rows = [["Fecha","Entrada","Salida","Trabajado","Balance","Tipo evento","Horario/Horas","Nota"]]; data.records.filter(r => r.empId === id).forEach(r => { const w = r.checkOut ? diffMin(r.checkIn, r.checkOut) : null; const db = w !== null ? w - getExpectedMin(emp, r.date) : null; rows.push([fmtDate(r.checkIn), fmtTime(r.checkIn), r.checkOut ? fmtTime(r.checkOut) : "En turno", w !== null ? `${Math.floor(w/60)}h ${w%60}m` : "–", db !== null ? toHHMM(db) : "–", "", "", ""]); }); data.events.filter(e => e.empId === id).forEach(e => { const hs = e.timeFrom && e.timeTo ? `${e.timeFrom}–${e.timeTo}${e.hours ? ` (${e.hours})` : ""}` : e.hours || ""; rows.push([e.date, "", "", "", "", EVENT_TYPES[e.type]?.label || e.type, hs, e.note || ""]); }); exportCSV(rows, `reporte-${emp.name.replace(/\s/g, "-")}.csv`); }; const doMonthCSV = () => { const rows = [["Empleado","Días","Trabajado","Esperado","Extras","A deber","Francos","Vacaciones","Trámites","Solicitudes"]]; data.employees.forEach(emp => { const mrecs = getMonthRecs(emp.id, repYear, repMonth); const mevts = getMonthEvts(emp.id, repYear, repMonth); const s = getStats(emp.id, [...data.records.filter(r => !mrecs.includes(r)), ...mrecs], [...data.events.filter(e => !mevts.includes(e)), ...mevts]); // recalculate just for this month const recs = mrecs.filter(r => r.checkIn && r.checkOut); const evts = mevts; const exemptDates = new Set(); evts.filter(e => EXEMPT_TYPES.has(e.type)).forEach(e => { if (e.dateTo) { let cur = new Date(e.date+"T12:00:00"), end = new Date(e.dateTo+"T12:00:00"); while(cur<=end){exemptDates.add(cur.toISOString().slice(0,10));cur.setDate(cur.getDate()+1);} } else if(e.date) exemptDates.add(e.date); }); let worked=0, expected=0; recs.forEach(r => { worked += diffMin(r.checkIn, r.checkOut); if (!exemptDates.has(r.date)) expected += getExpectedMin(emp, r.date); }); const bal = worked - expected; const ct = t => evts.filter(e => e.type === t).length; rows.push([emp.name, recs.length, `${Math.floor(worked/60)}h ${worked%60}m`, `${Math.floor(expected/60)}h ${expected%60}m`, toHHMM(Math.max(0,bal)), toHHMM(-Math.min(0,bal)), ct("franco"), ct("vacation"), ct("tramite"), ct("solicitud")]); }); exportCSV(rows, `mensual-${MONTHS[repMonth]}-${repYear}.csv`); }; const empDetail = selEmp ?
